/**********************************************************************************\
 *  Wks databases, DDL create script (WKS - 20221213093208)
 *  
 *  create all databases and table
 *
 *  NOTES:
 *
 *  in order to find the folder paths for DATA & LOG use the following:
 *  declare @a varchar(256); set @a = convert(varchar, serverproperty('InstanceDefaultDataPath'))
 *  declare @b varchar(256); set @b = convert(varchar, serverproperty('InstanceDefaultLogPath'))
 *
 *  ntext , text, and image data types will be removed in a future version of Microsoft SQL Server
 *  Avoid using these data types, use nvarchar(max), varchar(max), and varbinary(max) instead
 *  In SQL server 2005 new datatypes were introduced: varchar(max) and nvarchar(max)
 *  They have the advantages of the old text type: they can contain op to 2GB of data,
 *  but they also have most of the advantages of varchar and nvarchar.
 *  Among these advantages are the ability to use string manipulation functions such as substring().
 *
\***********************************************************************************/
